<td>3 pieces
<dl><dd><b>1. Gigues</b>
</dd><dd><b>2. Ibéria</b>
<dl><dd>I. Par les rues et les chemins
</dd><dd>II. Les parfums de la nuit
</dd><dd>III. Le matin d'un jour de fête
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><b>3. Rondes de printemps</b>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>

</th>
<td>1905-12
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1910-02-20 (Ibéria)
<dl><dd>Paris. Orchestre de Concerts Colonne, <a href="/wiki/Category:Piern%C3%A9,_Gabriel" title="Category:Pierné, Gabriel">Gabriel Pierné</a> (conductor)
</dd></dl>
<p>1910-03-02 (Rondes de printemps)
</p>
<dl><dd>Paris, Salle Gaveau. Orchestre de Concerts Durand, Claude Debussy (conductor)
</dd></dl>
<p>1913-01-26 (Complete)
</p>
<dl><dd>Paris. Orchestre de Concerts Colonne, Claude Debussy (conductor)
</dd></dl>

<td>Emma Debussy

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Orchestra:</i> (different for each piece) <span class="expandline">
<dl><dd><i>Gigues</i>
<dl><dd>2 flutes, 2 piccolos, 2 oboes, oboe d'amore, English horn, 
<dl><dd>3 clarinets (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>), bass clarinet (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>), 3 bassoons, contrabassoon
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>4 horns (F), 4 trumpets (C), 3 trombones
</dd><dd>timpani, cymbals, snare drum, xylophone
</dd><dd>celesta, 2 harps, strings
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Iberia</i>
<dl><dd>3 flutes (3rd also piccolo), piccolo, 2 oboes, English horn, 
<dl><dd>3 clarinets (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>, A), 3 bassoons, contrabassoon
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>4 horns (F), 3 trumpets (C), 3 trombones, tuba
</dd><dd>timpani, tambourine, castanets, cymbals, snare drum, xylophone, bells (3)
</dd><dd>celesta, 2 harps, strings
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Rondes de printemps</i>
<dl><dd>3 flutes (3rd also piccolo), 2 oboes, English horn, 3 clarinets (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>, A), 
<dl><dd>3 bassoons, contrabassoon
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>4 horns (F)
</dd><dd>timpani, triangle, tambourine, cymbals
</dd><dd>celesta, 2 harps, strings </span>
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
